What Greek warrior traded armor with a Trojan warrior during the battle, because they had past host-guest ties? ANSWER:DIOMEDES BONUS:Who was the Trojan warrior that Diomedes exchanged with? ANSWER:GLAUCUS BONUS:Who was Diomedes’ father that hosted Glaucus’ father? ANSWER:TYDEUS 
What god was thought to be born from Chaos by Hesiod, but is more commonly known to be the son of Aphrodite and Ares? ANSWER:EROS BONUS:According to Hesiod, from what was Aphrodite born? ANSWER:(SEA) FOAM/DISMEMBERED GENITALS OF URANUS BONUS: However, Homer writes that Aphrodite was conceived naturally. Who were her parents? ANSWER: ZEUS and DIONE 
In Book VI of Ovid’s Metamorphoses, what goddess tries to drink at the pond, but is harassed by the Lycian peasants? ANSWER:LATONA (MODERATOR SHOULD NOT ACCEPT LETO) BONUS:Into what animal did Latona turn the indignant peasants? ANSWER:FROGS BONUS:Where did Latona find temporary refuge to give birth? ANSWER:DELOS 
In Aeschylus’ The Libation Bearers, who leaves two locks of his hair on the tomb of Agamemnon? ANSWER:ORESTES BONUS:Who recognized the locks of hair and the footprints of Orestes? ANSWER:ELECTRA BONUS:What childhood friend accompanies Orestes to Mycenae? ANSWER:PYLADES 
Appearing in Ovid’s Heroides, which mythological figure from Abydos sought his lover who was a priestess of Aphrodite by swimming across the Hellespont, but drowned? ANSWER:LEANDER BONUS:Give the name of Leander’s lover. ANSWER:HERO BONUS: In what town did Hero dwell? ANSWER:SESTOS 
What woman, the daughter of Creon, was killed along with her three children by her husband, Heracles, who had been sent into a fit of madness? ANSWER:MEGARA BONUS:Who cured the madness of Heracles with hellebore? ANSWER:ANTIKYREUS BONUS: Heracles was not his born name, but a name given to him by the Oracle. What was his original name? ANSWER:ALCIDES/ALCAEUS 
According to Ovid, what son of Oeneus [OY-NAY-US] and Althea had his life connected to the status of a log? ANSWER:MELEAGER BONUS:Why did Althea throw the log into the fire knowing full well that it would kill her son? ANSWER:MELEAGER HAD KILLED HIS UNCLES, ALTHEA’S BROTHERS BONUS:Who were Althea’s brothers? ANSWER:TOXEUS and PLEXIPPUS 
What food did Hades deceive Persephone into eating, resulting in her imprisonment in the Underworld for a portion of the year? ANSWER:POMEGRANATE (SEEDS) BONUS:What group of daughters were Persephone’s companions and were transformed into winged creatures to search for their lost friend? ANSWER:SIRENS/DAUGHTERS OF ACHELOUS BONUS: Triptolemus, who presides over the sowing of grain-seed and the milling of wheat, is the demigod of what cult of Demeter near Athens? ANSWER:ELEUSINIAN (MYSTERIES) 
What faithful swine-herder of Odysseus helped his master defeat the suitors? ANSWER:EUMAEUS BONUS:What goat-herder was the complete opposite of Eumaeus and sided with the suitors? ANSWER:MELANTHEUS BONUS:What bard entertained the suitors, but he was spared by Odysseus? ANSWER:PHEMIUS 
Who was the first ally of Zeus in the war against the Titans? ANSWER:STYX BONUS:What was Styx’s reward for being the first ally? ANSWER:THE GODS SWEAR UPON HER BONUS: How many times does the river Styx flow around the Underworld? ANSWER:SEVEN 
What proud daughter of Idmon boasted that her skill in weaving equaled the skill of the goddess of the art herself, Athena? ANSWER:ARACHNE BONUS:Arachne in her weaving depicts the gods seducing various mortals. Antiope the daughter of Nycteus and mother of twins was seduced by Zeus in what form? ANSWER:SATYR BONUS: From what city in Lydia did Arachne hail? ANSWER:COLOPHON 
What fire-breathing creature stole Geryon’s cattle from Hercules and hid them in his cave? ANSWER:CACUS BONUS:According to Vergil, who is Cacus’s father? ANSWER:VULCAN BONUS: Who tells this story in the Aeneid? ANSWER:EVANDER 
Who of the following characters was not a child of Cadmus and Harmonia: Polydorus, Melicertes, Agave, Semele and Autonoë? ANSWER:MELICERTES BONUS:Melicertes was the son of one of Cadmus’ daughters. What was her name? ANSWER:INO BONUS:Athamas, Ino’s husband, was driven mad by Hera. He chased Ino and their son Melicertes to the sea where they were changed into sea divinities. What was Ino’s new name? ANSWER:LEUCOTHEA 
What daughter of Erectheus was impregnated by Apollo, abandoned her child Ion and unknowingly encountered him grown up when visiting Delphi? ANSWER:CREUSA BONUS:Who was Creusa’s husband who was seeking when he would have a child from Delphi? ANSWER:XUTHUS BONUS:Who reveals their relationship to Creusa and Ion? ANSWER:ATHENA 
After the disastrous flood that killed the world’s population, Deucalion and Pyrrha found themselves to be all alone. To what god or goddess – the present oracle - did they pray for guidance? ANSWER:THEMIS BONUS:Themis told them to “toss the bones of the great mother behind your back.” Please interpret the oracle’s words. ANSWER:THROW STONES BEHIND THEIR BACK BONUS:Deucalion and Pyrrha succeeded in repopulating the earth. The couple also had a son whose name is used to call the Greeks as a collective people. Name this son. ANSWER:HELLEN 
What one eyed monster loved the beautiful Nereid Galatea, and in an attempt to woo her, combed his hair with a rake and shaved his beard with a scythe? ANSWER:POLYPHEMUS BONUS:Galatea rejected Polyphemus in favor of what beautiful youth? ANSWER:ACIS BONUS:In a rage, Polyphemus crushed Acis under a large stone. Galatea decided to turn the blood of her lover into what? ANSWER: WATER/STREAM/RIVER 
What son of Eurynome was framed by Sthenoboea and was sent to the court of King Iobates [EE-OH-BAH-TAYS]? ANSWER:BELLEROPHON BONUS:By what other name is Sthenoboea, the daughter of Antias is known? ANSWER:ANTIA BONUS: Name any one of Bellerophon’s children. ANSWER:LAODAMEIA/HIPPOLOCUS/ISANDROS 
Whose murder at the court of King Aegeas of Athens prompted Minos to demand an annual tribute of youths and maidens to be fed to the Minotaur? ANSWER:ANDROGEUS BONUS: By what other name is the Minotaur know? ANSWER:ASTERION BONUS: Who was Minos’s half-brother, who was his fellow judge in the Underworld? ANSWER:AEACUS 
Whose daughters were punished with madness for resisting the worship of Dionysus? ANSWER:PROETUS’ BONUS:Which seer cured his daughters’ madness? ANSWER:MELAMPUS BONUS:What other group of daughters also avoided the worship of Dionysus and were turned into bats? MINYAS’ ANSWER:INTERMEDIATE 
What son of Neleus was given the power of shape-shifting, which he used in the battle against Hercules? ANSWER:PERICLYMENUS BONUS:Into what animal form was Periclymenus transformed when Hercules shot him down with an arrow? ANSWER:EAGLE BONUS:What brother of Periclymenus had been telling this story of the battle against Hercules? ANSWER:NESTOR 
What daughter of Perses and Asteria was the goddess of witchcraft and crossroads? ANSWER:HEKATE BONUS: Name a goddess who was associated or said to be the same as Hekate. ANSWER:ARTEMIS/SELENE BONUS:Who princess of Colchis had prayed to Hekate for guidance in assisting Jason? ANSWER:MEDEA 
What king was going to seek guidance from the Delphic Oracle, but was caught in a storm and died unbeknownst to his wife? ANSWER:CEYX BONUS:Who was Ceyx’s wife? ANSWER:ALCYONE BONUS:Who, out of pity, eventually told Alcyone the fate of her husband through a dream? ANSWER:JUNO 
What son of Nestor guided Telemachus to his home and to Menelaus’ home? ANSWER:PEISISTRATUS BONUS:When Telemachus visited Menelaus’ home, who had given him a soothing drink using an Egyptian drug? ANSWER:HELEN BONUS:Why had Telemachus ventured from Ithaca to visit Nestor and Menelaus? ANSWER:HE WAS SEEKING INFORMATION ON HIS FATHER’S WHEREABOUTS
